 The Abhinav Bindra-led National Rifle Association of India (NRAI) review committee not only targeted underperforming shooters but also spared the coaches and federation for the poor performance of shooters in the Rio Olympics and recommended radical changes
 
 samiti ne 2012 landan khelon main kaansya padak jeetne vaale gagan naarang, hina siddhu or yonika paul kii aalochana kii he
 The four-member committee has given a 36-page hard report reviewing the performance
 asian khelon kii purv swarna padak vijeta tennis khilaadi manisha malhotra isaki samanvayak hai
 The committee has concluded that consecutive medals in shooting since the Athens Olympic 2004 made everyone involved with the Games bewildered
 report ke anusaar, ‘sabhi ne soch liya ki apane aap hi pragati hoti rahegi or yah sunishchit karnaa bhul gaye ki swasth prakriya honi chahie
 ' isamen kaha gaya, ‘samiti kii charchaa kaa nishkarsh nikaalte hue kaha ja saktaa he ki rio olympic main safalataa kaa formula galat tha or bhartiya nishanebaaji pichley kuch varshon se bhagya ke sahare rahi he lekin isamen koi shaq nahin ki kuch shandaar pratibhavan khilaadiyon se madad mili he
 'none of the 12 shooters from India who qualified for the Rio Olympics were able to win a medal, after which a committee was formed to review the performance
 bindra kaa 10 meter air rifl main chauthe sthaan par rahanaa bharat kaa nishanebaaji main sarvshereshth pradarshan tha
 The committee unanimously stated in its report that a change in Indian shooting was needed
 ravaiye, nitiyon or yojanaon main badlaav kii jarurat he jisase ki pratibha ko swasth maahaul main panpane kaa mauka mili
 The committee also said that the 'moves' in the Indian Games are overshadowed
 samiti ne gagan naarang or hina siddhu jaise senior khilaadiyon ke alaava yonika paal jaisi ubhartee hui nishanebaaj ko bhi nahin bakhsha
 Heena was criticized for making her husband Ronk Pandit a personal coach and the committee said that she would have to take some tough decisions regarding her competition
 samiti ne kaha, ‘shaayad use training varsh (2017) kaa istemaal yah spasht karne ke liye karnaa chahie ki 25 meter sports pistal asal main unki pasandida 10 meter air pistal ko sahyog detii he yaa nahin
 There is clearly complexity
 rashtriya coach pavel smirnov ke saath koi sahyog nahin tha jisase sthiti main madad nahin mili
 Regarding Ionika, the panel believes that this talented young shooter was not able to make his plans
 samiti ne kaha ki yonika ne vittiya phaayde ke liye thomas farnic ko coach or suma shirur ko menter dikhaaya lekin samiti ke saamne pesh report or dastavej sabit karte hai ki suma purnakalik coach thim or olympic kii taiyaari ke prayaason main puri eemaandaaree nahin dikhaai gai
 Noting up to strong contender Jitu Rai's expectations, the committee said that the pistol shooter did not get the right expertise and could not form a working relationship with foreign coach Smirnov
 prakaash nanjappa ke liye yojana nahin bana paane ke liye smirnov kii bhi aalochana kii gai
 The committee also strongly criticized Narang, who won the bronze medal at the 2012 London Games, saying that the shooter landed with a heel injury in the Games and did not uphold the training scheme he had set for himself
 samiti ne kaha, ‘coach stenislas lepids ko yakeen tha ki naarang unke training kaarykram par nahin chal rahe hai jisaki soochna kai baar enareai ko di gai
 However no action was taken
 fitness ke mudde ko nanjarandaaj kiya gaya or naarang ke edi main chot ke saath olympic main jane ko lekar enareai andhere main tha
 The committee also strongly criticized the rifle shooter Apoorvi Chandela
 tippaniyan The committee said that it believes that Coach Lepidus' claim that Apoorvi had to fight to get funds for training is confusing
 tops yojana main apurvi kaa maamla sabase pehle sweekruti paane waalon main shaamil tha
 However, funds could not be released until Apoorvi's training plan and program were not handed over
 bindra ke chauthe sthaan par rahane ke liye bhagya ko jimmedaar tehraate hue samiti ne kaha ki yah shandaar kariyar kaa acha ant tha, haalanki isamen pariktha jaise ant kii kami thi
